#	Spelling Rules:
#	Kan-on Reading preferably, else it's Go-on. Longer Vowels are to be shortened except extremely short names. So Ooshimi = Oshimi, Hakoguchii = Hakoguchi etc.
#	Avoid Z in San/Mountain. So not Fuzan but Fusan.
#############
